If you set the "Multi Character Mode" option to
ON, you will be able to control 2-4 planes simul-
-taneously. In the Character Selection screen,
 press the Start Button to add a plane to your
 party. During the game, press the Change Butto-
-n to change the formation of your party.
You can enable/disable the Character Demo Event.
If you set this option to OFF, the character de-
-mo sequence will not occur.
